GameCombat.java:245:	public static boolean updateWave() {

GameCombat.java:247:			// if the wave is done, move to next wave
GameCombat.java:248:			wave++;

GameCombat.java:256:	public static boolean handleCharacterInput(int userID, char typed) {
GameCombat.java:257:		boolean hasKilledFish = false;
GameCombat.java:259:		Iterator<ActiveFish> it = swimmingFishes.iterator();
GameCombat.java:260:		while (it.hasNext()) {
GameCombat.java:261:			ActiveFish f = it.next();
GameCombat.java:262:			if (f.word.charAt(f.lettersTyped) == Character.toUpperCase(typed)) {
GameCombat.java:263:				// if you typed the next letter
GameCombat.java:264:				f.lettersTyped += 1;
GameCombat.java:266:				if (f.lettersTyped == f.word.length()) {
GameCombat.java:267:					// if you typed the last letter of the word
GameCombat.java:268:					
GameCombat.java:269:					// Update Stats
GameCombat.java:270:					lastFish = new ActiveFish(f.type, f.word, f.lane, f.x);
GameCombat.java:271:					
GameCombat.java:272:					gold += f.type.coins; 
GameCombat.java:273:					kills += 1;
GameCombat.java:274:					totalChars += f.word.length();
GameCombat.java:276:					// Record specific fish kill in DiscoveredFishes
GameCombat.java:277:					updateDiscoveredFishes(userID, f.type.id);
GameCombat.java:279:					remainingInWave -= 1;
GameCombat.java:280:					
GameCombat.java:281:					// remove completed fish from list
GameCombat.java:282:					it.remove();
GameCombat.java:284:					if (swimmingFishes.size() == 0) {
GameCombat.java:285:						combatTime += System.currentTimeMillis() - combatStart;
GameCombat.java:286:						isCombat = false;
GameCombat.java:287:					}
GameCombat.java:289:					
GameCombat.java:290:					hasKilledFish = true;
GameCombat.java:291:				}
GameCombat.java:292:			}	else if (f.word.charAt(0) == Character.toUpperCase(typed)) {
GameCombat.java:293:				f.lettersTyped = 1;
GameCombat.java:294:			} else {
GameCombat.java:295:				// if you did not type the next letter
GameCombat.java:296:				f.lettersTyped = 0;
GameCombat.java:297:			}
GameCombat.java:298:		}
GameCombat.java:300:		return hasKilledFish;
GameCombat.java:301:	}
GameCombat.java:303:	public static boolean moveFishesAndCheckStickmanCollision(int userID, int pondID) {
GameCombat.java:304:		for (ActiveFish f : swimmingFishes) {
GameCombat.java:305:			// check stickman collision
GameCombat.java:306:			if (f.x < STICKMAN_COL + STICKMAN_WIDTH) { 
GameCombat.java:307:				// if stickman gets touch, end game
GameCombat.java:308:				saveResults(userID, pondID, gold, kills, totalChars, startTime, wave);
GameCombat.java:309:				return true; 
GameCombat.java:310:			}
GameCombat.java:311:			
GameCombat.java:312:			// move this fish
GameCombat.java:313:			f.x -= 1;	
GameCombat.java:314:		}
GameCombat.java:315:		
GameCombat.java:316:		// stickman was not touched
GameCombat.java:317:		return false;
GameCombat.java:318:	}
GameCombat.java:320:	public static FishType getRandomFishType() {
GameCombat.java:321:		FishType selected = null;
GameCombat.java:323:		float dice = new Random().nextFloat() * totalSpawnRateWeight;
GameCombat.java:325:		float cumulative = 0;
GameCombat.java:326:		for (FishType ft : fishSpecies) {
GameCombat.java:327:			cumulative += ft.spawnRate;
GameCombat.java:328:			if (dice <= cumulative) {
GameCombat.java:329:				selected = ft;
GameCombat.java:330:				break; 
GameCombat.java:331:			}
GameCombat.java:332:		}
GameCombat.java:334:		return selected;
GameCombat.java:335:	}
GameCombat.java:337:	public static void spawnFishIfPossible() {
GameCombat.java:338:		if (numFishMovesBeforeNextSpawn > 0) {
GameCombat.java:339:			// if must wait a number of moves before spaqn
GameCombat.java:340:			numFishMovesBeforeNextSpawn -= 1;
GameCombat.java:341:			return;
GameCombat.java:342:		}
GameCombat.java:344:		// if you have waited a number of moves, you can now spawn a fish
GameCombat.java:345:		if (remainingInWave > swimmingFishes.size() && !fishSpecies.isEmpty()) {
GameCombat.java:346:			// if the wave still has a fish to spawn
GameCombat.java:347:			FishType selected = getRandomFishType();
GameCombat.java:349:			if (selected == null) {
GameCombat.java:350:				return;
GameCombat.java:351:			}
GameCombat.java:353:			String word = dictionary.get(new Random().nextInt(dictionary.size()));
GameCombat.java:354:			int spawnX = screenWidth - RIGHT_MARGIN - (selected.head.length() + word.length() + selected.tail.length());
GameCombat.java:356:			// check if a fish can spawn on this lane
GameCombat.java:357:			boolean clear = true;
GameCombat.java:358:			for (ActiveFish f : swimmingFishes) {
GameCombat.java:359:				int spawnFishLeftX = spawnX;
GameCombat.java:360:				int thisFishRightX = f.x + f.getFullWidth();
GameCombat.java:361:				if (f.lane == currentSpawnLane && spawnFishLeftX - thisFishRightX < MIN_FISH_GAP) {
GameCombat.java:362:					// if a fish is blocking this lane
GameCombat.java:363:					clear = false;
GameCombat.java:364:				}
GameCombat.java:365:			}
GameCombat.java:366:			if (clear) {
GameCombat.java:367:				// if a fish can spawn
GameCombat.java:368:				if (swimmingFishes.size() == 0) {
GameCombat.java:369:					combatStart = System.currentTimeMillis();
GameCombat.java:370:					isCombat = true;
GameCombat.java:371:				}
GameCombat.java:373:				swimmingFishes.add(new ActiveFish(selected, word, currentSpawnLane, spawnX));
GameCombat.java:374:				
GameCombat.java:375:				// wait again a number of moves, after spawning a fish
GameCombat.java:376:				numFishMovesBeforeNextSpawn = new Random().nextInt(Math.max(4, 10 - wave) + 1);
GameCombat.java:377:				currentSpawnLane = new Random().nextInt(LANE_COUNT);
GameCombat.java:379:			} 
GameCombat.java:380:		}
GameCombat.java:381:	}
GameCombat.java:383:	public static boolean updateCombat(int userID, int pondID) {
GameCombat.java:384:		boolean isDead = false;
GameCombat.java:386:		now = System.currentTimeMillis();
GameCombat.java:387:		if (now - lastTick > (secPerChar * 1000)) { 
GameCombat.java:388:			// if the fishes must now move based on speed
GameCombat.java:389:			isDead = moveFishesAndCheckStickmanCollision(userID, pondID);
GameCombat.java:390:			spawnFishIfPossible();
GameCombat.java:392:			lastTick = now;
GameCombat.java:393:		}
GameCombat.java:394:		sec = Math.max(1, (now - startTime - pausedTime) / 1000);
GameCombat.java:396:		if (isCombat) {
GameCombat.java:397:			wpm = (totalChars / 5.0) / (Math.max(1, (now - combatStart + combatTime) / 1000) / 60.0);
GameCombat.java:398:		} else {
GameCombat.java:399:			wpm = (totalChars / 5.0) / (Math.max(1, combatTime / 1000) / 60.0);
GameCombat.java:400:		}
GameCombat.java:402:		return isDead;
GameCombat.java:403:	} 
GameCombat.java:405:	public static void start(Screen screen, int userID, int pondID) {

GameCombat.java:411:		try {
GameCombat.java:412:			while (!isDead) {
GameCombat.java:413:				isDead = updateCombat(userID, pondID);
GameCombat.java:414:			}
GameCombat.java:415:		} catch (Exception error) {
GameCombat.java:416:			error.printStackTrace();
GameCombat.java:417:		}
GameCombat.java:419:	}
